ty=`
varying vec3 vWorldPosition;
varying vec3 vDirection;

void main() {
    vec4 worldPosition = modelMatrix * vec4(position, 1.0);
    vWorldPosition = worldPosition.xyz;
    vDirection = normalize(position);
    
    gl_Position = projectionMatrix * modelViewMatrix * vec4(position, 1.0);
    gl_Position.z = gl_Position.w; // Force to far plane
}
`,ny=`
uniform float uTime; // 0.0 to 1.0 day cycle
uniform vec3 uSunPosition;
uniform float uSunSize;
uniform vec3 uSunColor;
uniform vec3 uMoonColor;
uniform float uMoonSize;
uniform float uStarRotation; // Star field rotation angle

// Sky colors for different times
uniform vec3 uDayTopColor;
uniform vec3 uDayBottomColor;
uniform vec3 uSunsetTopColor;
uniform vec3 uSunsetBottomColor;
uniform vec3 uNightTopColor;
uniform vec3 uNightBottomColor;

varying vec3 vWorldPosition;
varying vec3 vDirection;

// Simple noise for stars
float hash(vec2 p) {
    return fract(sin(dot(p, vec2(127.1, 311.7))) * 43758.5453);
}

// Rotate a 2D point around the origin
vec2 rotate2D(vec2 p, float angle) {
    float s = sin(angle);
    float c = cos(angle);
    return vec2(p.x * c - p.y * s, p.x * s + p.y * c);
}

vec3 getSkyColor(float time, float height) {
    vec3 topColor, bottomColor;
    
    if (time < 0.23) {
        // Night (0.0 - 0.23) - much longer night
        topColor = uNightTopColor;
        bottomColor = uNightBottomColor;
    } else if (time < 0.25) {
        // Dawn transition (0.23 - 0.25) - very short dawn
        float t = (time - 0.23) / 0.005;
        topColor = mix(uNightTopColor, uSunsetTopColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
        bottomColor = mix(uNightBottomColor, uSunsetBottomColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
    } else if (time < 0.27) {
        // Sunrise (0.25 - 0.27) - very short sunrise
        float t = (time - 0.25) / 0.005;
        topColor = mix(uSunsetTopColor, uDayTopColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
        bottomColor = mix(uSunsetBottomColor, uDayBottomColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
    } else if (time < 0.73) {
        // Day (0.27 - 0.73) - longer day
        topColor = uDayTopColor;
        bottomColor = uDayBottomColor;
    } else if (time < 0.75) {
        // Sunset start (0.73 - 0.75) - very short sunset start
        float t = (time - 0.73) / 0.005;
        topColor = mix(uDayTopColor, uSunsetTopColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
        bottomColor = mix(uDayBottomColor, uSunsetBottomColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
    } else if (time < 0.755) {
        // Sunset (0.75 - 0.77) - very short sunset
        topColor = uSunsetTopColor;
        bottomColor = uSunsetBottomColor;
    } else {
        // Dusk to night (0.77 - 1.0) - longer night transition
        float t = (time - 0.77) / 0.005;
        topColor = mix(uSunsetTopColor, uNightTopColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
        bottomColor = mix(uSunsetBottomColor, uNightBottomColor, smoothstep(0.0, 1.0, t));
    }
    
    // Create gradient from bottom to top
    float gradient = clamp((height + 0.2) * 1.2, 0.0, 1.0);
    return mix(bottomColor, topColor, gradient);
}

void main() {
    vec3 direction = normalize(vDirection);
    float height = direction.y;
    
    // Get base sky color
    vec3 skyColor = getSkyColor(uTime, height);
    
    // Calculate sun position and visibility
    vec3 sunDir = normalize(uSunPosition);
    
    // Fixed square sun - use angular distance instead of screen projection
    vec3 sunRight = normalize(cross(sunDir, vec3(0.0, 1.0, 0.0)));
    vec3 sunUp = normalize(cross(sunRight, sunDir));
    
    float sunDotX = abs(dot(direction - sunDir, sunRight));
    float sunDotY = abs(dot(direction - sunDir, sunUp));
    float sunMask = step(sunDotX, uSunSize) * step(sunDotY, uSunSize);
    
    // Only show sun when it's above horizon and during day times
    float sunAboveHorizon = step(0.0, sunDir.y);
    
    // Sun visibility: gradual fade in/out over longer periods
    float sunVisibility = 0.0;
    if (uTime >= 0.15 && uTime <= 0.85) {
        sunVisibility = sunAboveHorizon;
        // Much longer, smoother fade periods
        if (uTime < 0.35) {
            // Fade in from 0.15 to 0.35 (longer sunrise period)
            sunVisibility *= smoothstep(0.15, 0.35, uTime);
        } else if (uTime > 0.65) {
            // Fade out from 0.65 to 0.85 (longer sunset period)
            sunVisibility *= smoothstep(0.85, 0.65, uTime);
        }
        
        // Additional smooth fade based on sun height above horizon
        float horizonFade = smoothstep(-0.1, 0.1, sunDir.y);
        sunVisibility *= horizonFade;
    }
    
    // Sun glow effect (only when sun is visible and above horizon)
    float sunDistance = distance(direction, sunDir);
    float sunGlow = (1.0 - smoothstep(0.0, 0.4, sunDistance)) * sunAboveHorizon;
    sunGlow = pow(sunGlow, 3.0);
    
    // Moon position (opposite of sun)
    vec3 moonDir = -sunDir;
    
    // Fixed square moon - same technique as sun
    vec3 moonRight = normalize(cross(moonDir, vec3(0.0, 1.0, 0.0)));
    vec3 moonUp = normalize(cross(moonRight, moonDir));
    
    float moonDotX = abs(dot(direction - moonDir, moonRight));
    float moonDotY = abs(dot(direction - moonDir, moonUp));
    float moonMask = step(moonDotX, uMoonSize) * step(moonDotY, uMoonSize);
    
    // Only show moon when it's above horizon and during night
    float moonAboveHorizon = step(0.0, moonDir.y);
    
    // Moon visibility: gradual fade in/out over longer periods
    float moonVisibility = 0.0;
    if (uTime <= 0.35 || uTime >= 0.65) {
        moonVisibility = moonAboveHorizon;
        // Much smoother, longer fade periods
        if (uTime <= 0.35 && uTime >= 0.15) {
            // Fade out from 0.15 to 0.35 (dawn period)
            moonVisibility *= smoothstep(0.35, 0.15, uTime);
        } else if (uTime >= 0.65 && uTime <= 0.85) {
            // Fade in from 0.65 to 0.85 (dusk period)
            moonVisibility *= smoothstep(0.65, 0.85, uTime);
        } else if (uTime <= 0.15 || uTime >= 0.85) {
            // Fully visible during deep night
            moonVisibility *= 1.0;
        }
        
        // Additional smooth fade based on moon height above horizon
        float horizonFade = smoothstep(-0.1, 0.1, moonDir.y);
        moonVisibility *= horizonFade;
    }
    
    // Add rotating stars during night
    vec3 finalColor = skyColor;
    if (uTime < 0.3 || uTime > 0.7) {
        // Use the same UV mapping approach as Godot for proper star distribution
        // Project the sky direction onto a 2D plane (like Godot's EYEDIR.xz / sqrt(EYEDIR.y))
        vec2 skyUV = direction.xz / sqrt(abs(direction.y) + 0.01);
        
        // Rotate the UV coordinates using the same method as Godot
        float cosR = cos(uStarRotation);
        float sinR = sin(uStarRotation);
        
        vec2 rotatedStarUV = vec2(
            skyUV.x * cosR - skyUV.y * sinR,
            skyUV.x * sinR + skyUV.y * cosR
        );
        
        // Scale for star density
        rotatedStarUV *= 50.0;
        
        // Use the 2D hash on the rotated UV coordinates
        float starField = hash(floor(rotatedStarUV));
        float starBrightness = 0.0;
        
        if (uTime < 0.25 || uTime > 0.75) {
            starBrightness = 1.0;
        } else if (uTime < 0.3) {
            starBrightness = smoothstep(0.3, 0.25, uTime);
        } else if (uTime > 0.7) {
            starBrightness = smoothstep(0.7, 0.75, uTime);
        }
        
        // Only show stars above horizon and not too close to sun/moon
        if (starField > 0.998 && direction.y > 0.1) {
            // Dim stars near sun and moon (using original direction for proximity)
            float sunProximity = 1.0 - smoothstep(0.1, 0.3, distance(direction, sunDir));
            float moonProximity = 1.0 - smoothstep(0.1, 0.3, distance(direction, moonDir));
            float celestialDimming = 1.0 - max(sunProximity * sunVisibility, moonProximity * moonVisibility);
            
            finalColor += vec3(1.0) * starBrightness * 0.8 * celestialDimming;
        }
    }
    
    // Apply sun glow (warm orange during sunset)
    if (sunVisibility > 0.0) {
        vec3 glowColor = uSunColor;
        if (uTime > 0.6 && uTime < 0.8) {
            // Extra warm during sunset
            glowColor = mix(uSunColor, vec3(1.0, 0.4, 0.1), 0.7);
        }
        finalColor = mix(finalColor, glowColor, sunGlow * sunVisibility * 0.3);
    }
    
    // Add sun disk
    finalColor = mix(finalColor, uSunColor, sunMask * sunVisibility);
    
    // Add moon
    finalColor = mix(finalColor, uMoonColor, moonMask * moonVisibility);
    
    // Boost contrast and saturation
    finalColor = pow(finalColor, vec3(0.9));
    
    gl_FragColor = vec4(finalColor, 1.0);
}
